Foreign Minister Uchida's Speech on Diplomatic Policy

Claims that Supporting the Puppet State Can Lead to Peace in the East

Consolidating Our National Defense is Falsely Accused as Aggression

Falsely Accuses Our Redification Attempt to Confuse World Public Opinion

(Tokyo) The House of Peers convened at 11:00 AM this morning. Foreign Minister Uchida delivered a speech on the government's diplomatic policy. The full text is as follows:

Regarding the Puppet State Incident

Based on its established policy, the Imperial Government signed a protocol with the "Manchukuo" government on September 15th of last year. The Imperial Government officially recognized "Manchukuo" as an independent state and stipulated that "Manchukuo" respect all treaty rights and interests of the Empire and its subjects within that country. Japan and "Manchukuo" agreed that everything concerning "Manchukuo" was related to the Empire's tranquility and security. It was stipulated that Imperial troops would be stationed within "Manchukuo" to jointly defend the country. As a result of signing this protocol, the foundation for protecting Japan's rights and interests in Manchuria and ensuring "Manchukuo" against internal and external threats has been established, and a powerful guarantee for maintaining peace in the East has been realized. "Manchukuo" has gradually developed since then. Local banditry has gradually been suppressed, and significant improvements in the domestic situation are cause for great joy. Needless to say, this state of affairs has the best influence on the country's commerce, trade, and finance. Therefore, both the people of Manchukuo and Japanese and foreign residents in Manchuria are enjoying prosperity. This fact practically proves the Japanese government's view that recognizing the new state is the only way to resolve the Manchurian problem and preserve peace in the Far East. In view of the above-mentioned good state and prosperity of Manchukuo, and the facts benefiting both Chinese and foreigners, I firmly believe that the League of Nations and the nations of the world will recognize the fair and appropriate attitude taken by the Empire. I have no doubt that the Chinese people will understand in the future that the best way to ensure peace in the Far East is for China, Japan, and Manchukuo to assist each other as independent countries.

Regarding the Jehol Problem

Regarding the Jehol problem, I would like to add a word. The Great Wall is the boundary between Manchuria and Mongolia and China, and there is no room for discussion when examining history. Furthermore, Jehol Province is a part of "Manchukuo," as is clear from the "Manchukuo" declaration. However, recently, not only are there those disrupting public order within Jehol Province, but also regular troops under Zhang Xueliang have crossed the border and invaded the province. The Japan-Manchukuo agreement stipulates that the two countries are jointly responsible for maintaining public order in the territory of Manchukuo. Therefore, the so-called Jehol problem is an internal problem of Manchukuo. At the same time, Japan has a major concern for this problem due to its treaty obligations.

Falsely Accuses Our Government of Being Chaotic

The Chinese political situation remains chaotic, and the anti-Japanese movement shows no signs of abating. It is reported that the Central Committee of the Kuomintang held a plenary meeting in Nanjing last December, submitting three active anti-Japanese proposals regarding military actions in the North China border region, assistance to the Northeast Volunteer Army, and the rejection of Japanese goods. Subsequently, according to various intelligence received from various parties, this active anti-Japanese proposal was indeed passed at the meeting. Recently, not only have Chinese troops gathered near the border between China and Manchukuo, but some have already invaded Jehol Province. The Imperial Government is now sincerely concerned about this state of affairs in China. Regarding the unfortunate consequences that may result from this situation, I must urge the Chinese government and its people to awaken to serious attention and introspection.

Regarding the Lytton Report

Regarding the so-called Lytton Report, which is related to the China-Japan problem, it was submitted to the Council of the League of Nations last October. The Imperial Government's opinion on it was also submitted to the Council in November. Both have already been made public. The content of the Japanese opinion comprehensively explains from various perspectives the Imperial Government's basic view that recognizing Manchukuo and helping its sound development is the only way to ensure peace in the Far East. The government will earnestly explain the gist of this opinion at the Council of the League of Nations, the General Assembly, and other opportunities for negotiation with the nations of the world. The Committee of Nineteen, which declared a temporary adjournment last December, reopened on the 16th of this month to continue discussing the China-Japan problem. The Japanese side has decided to strive in the future at every opportunity when the conference and other conferences of the League of Nations are held, to thoroughly assert the claims within the opinion. The Imperial Government has always sincerely assisted the cause of the League of Nations and strived to enhance its authority. It is fully prepared to cooperate in good faith with the League of Nations' efforts for peace and well-being in the Far East. It goes without saying. However, as stated in the Imperial Government's opinion, when the League of Nations deliberates on issues related to China, it should fully allow flexibility in the League Covenant due to the complexity and difficulty of the country's situation and the strong atmosphere of irregularities and characteristics. This is most necessary because the various principles and practices of international law that are implemented between ordinary countries are greatly altered and implemented in China. Therefore, it is not possible to make an exception solely based on the League Covenant. That is, if one wants to apply the Covenant in China based on precedents implemented in Europe according to the Covenant, the result will not conform to actual events. Not only will it instead make the situation worse, but it will also harm the authority of the League of Nations. This is extremely dangerous for world peace. To maintain peace in the Far East, on the one hand, the cooperation and collaboration of China, Japan, and Manchukuo are necessary, and on the other hand, smooth coordination between the three countries is also needed.

Regarding Diplomacy with Russia

Since the Manchurian Incident, the Soviet Russian Federation government has taken an extremely cautious attitude. Fortunately, no unpleasant incidents have occurred between Japan and Russia to date. This is cause for great joy for Japan, Manchukuo, and Russia. Recently, diplomatic relations between China and Russia have been restored. Therefore, there are often reports that the Redification movement throughout the Far East will become more active. Whether this observation is correct is temporarily not discussed. However, if the Redification forces increase along the Yangtze River and in southern China, where the Communist Party and Communist army are already active, this matter will be a major event for peace in the Far East. The Imperial Government will naturally pay close attention to its future. As for the issue of a non-aggression pact between Japan and Russia, it is the spirit of the Japan-Russia Basic Treaty established in Beiping the year before, and it is also stipulated by the Kellogg-Briand Pact, which both countries have signed. There is indeed a relationship of trust between the two countries, and there is absolutely no aggression. However, if one wants to add a formal non-aggression treaty to this spirit, stipulation, and this practical relationship, various views will naturally arise regarding the timing, method, and other aspects. Since the Russian government raised this issue last spring, there have been various discussions in various quarters. In view of the fact that there are various discussions on this issue, the Imperial Government believes that the time has not yet come to discuss or conclude a non-aggression treaty with the Russian government. Therefore, at the end of last year, it replied to the Soviet Russian government with this gist. Although the Japanese government replied to the Russian government in this way, it goes without saying that Japan has no intention of aggression against Soviet Russia. I believe that the Soviet Russian government will definitely not misunderstand this matter either.

Regarding the Disarmament Conference

The General Disarmament Conference was held in Geneva last February. Various important cases concerning the army, navy, and air force were discussed. However, the conference gathered representatives from countries around the world and was an unprecedentedly large conference. Because each country expects the safety of its national defense, and its interests are already very complex, no consensus has been seen yet. However, reducing armaments is a cause of peace and is not only one of the important tasks of the League of Nations but also one of the issues that countries around the world are most concerned about now. The Imperial Government's consistent policy of sincerely cooperating with these causes remains unchanged. Therefore, at this conference, the Japanese plenipotentiary, in cooperation with the representatives of various countries, will focus on the success of the conference. The intention of the Imperial Government in proposing a major reduction in world naval armaments last year is also for this purpose. The proposal advocates reducing the shape of various warships, completely abolishing aircraft carriers, reducing the number of A-class cruisers, and reducing the total tonnage of B-class cruisers and destroyers. According to this plan, the aircraft carriers and A-class cruisers of the five countries of Britain, Japan, the United States, France, and Italy could be reduced by about 1.3 million tons. The Japanese proposal takes the principle of reducing offensive power and increasing defensive power, which was passed by this conference, as its foundation. By adopting this principle, the superior naval power will naturally make greater sacrifices than the inferior naval power. If the same rate of reduction is applied to both countries, the safety of the inferior naval power will be greatly damaged. The Japanese proposal also carefully considers the claims of the countries concerned. If the countries fully study the Japanese proposal, I believe that the countries will definitely be able to understand its fair, rational, and practical claims. Looking at the current state of the world's financial circles, in addition to the fact that forty-four countries have suspended the gold standard and their trade has suffered losses due to the sharp decline in silver prices and the chaos in the foreign exchange market, countries are vying to set up restrictions on imports and exports, prohibit imports and exports, and raise tariffs, implementing the so-called isolationist policies in industry and trade. As a result, the great principle of free trade, which has always been developing healthily, has seen a major reversal. This is truly regrettable. However, recently, the enthusiasm for studying methods to eliminate global economic instability has been quite noticeable. Japan also has a policy of cooperating in carrying out such international efforts. Because the World Economic and Financial Conference, which will be held soon, is also based on the above-mentioned gist, the Japanese government often sends representatives to the preparatory committee of the conference to conduct various preliminary studies jointly with the countries. The various diplomatic issues currently facing us have been described above.

The So-called Government View

Finally, I would like to say a word about the view of the Imperial Government. It goes without saying that the fundamental meaning of the Empire's diplomacy lies in ensuring peace in the Far East and world peace. In the view of the Imperial Government, in view of the actual situation of the international community today, in order to achieve true peace, it is necessary to recognize the principled universality of the goal of maintaining peace. When applying it, it should be appropriate to the actual situation and allow appropriate flexibility. At the same time, it is most important to respect the forces in all parts of the world that can realize the maintenance of peace. For this reason, Japan recognizes the provisions in the League of Nations Charter that stipulate local understanding as a wise thing. At the same time, it recognizes the Empire's constructive power in the Far East as a realistic pillar for maintaining peace in that area, and it attempts to maintain peace in that area. The Empire has absolutely no territorial ambitions in any part of the world, nor does it want to create incidents against any country in the world. What the Empire is attempting is to ensure the Empire's lifeline based on national defense and justice, and at the same time, to work together with neighboring countries to ensure the tranquility of the Far East, in order to contribute to maintaining world peace. In the Far East, it wants to achieve this goal with its authority and strength. This is the belief of the Japanese people. The fundamental spirit of the Empire's diplomacy since the Meiji era lies in this. The attitude toward the aforementioned Manchurian problem, Japan-Russia relations, and the League of Nations is based on this spirit. Furthermore, the Empire's proposal to the Disarmament Conference also stems from the same spirit. Under the above-mentioned fundamental spirit, the Imperial Government intends to maintain the most friendly relations between countries, to promote the smoothness of trade and the integration of cultures, and to realize the higher ideals of mankind in the world. (21st Jiji News Agency Dispatch)

Paris Supports the League of Nations and Urges Effective Measures

Submits a Letter to the Executive Yuan Calling for Peace

(Paris) The chairman of the International Association of Academic Circles in Support of the League of Nations has recently written to the chairman of the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations regarding the Far East problem. This association has more than two million members. In 1931, due to the danger of the Sino-Japanese dispute, it wrote to the chairman of the Executive Yuan of the League of Nations, stating that if the Executive Yuan and the General Assembly cannot maintain peace and prevent war in the Far East, the credibility of the League of Nations may fall to the ground. This time, the association has made a final appeal to the Executive Yuan, stating that if the Sino-Japanese dispute cannot be resolved peacefully, it is imperative to take the necessary measures and sanctions to protect the dignity of the League of Nations Covenant. Current Affairs Commentary

The League of Nations' Mediation of Jehol is in Grave Danger

㈠ The So-Called Mediation of the League of Nations

The League of Nations' own imperfections are already known to the world, especially deeply understood by us. Although the United States of North America, which holds the reins of world finance, was the initiator, it has remained outside the League since its establishment. The Soviet Union, which occupies one-seventh of the world's land, is also not a member of the League. Among the major powers, the so-called loyal allies are Britain and France in Europe, and Japan in the East. The capitalist countries of continental Europe, with the exception of Germany and Italy, mostly follow the lead of Britain and France. Although Germany and Italy are each wielding their inherent abilities to strive for progress, Germany, which has been defeated for fifteen years, has been subjected to the restrictions of the Treaty of Versailles. Although it is now trying to revitalize itself, it has no surplus strength to interfere in foreign affairs due to the customs blockade by various countries and the困顿 of market decadence and rising unemployment. Italy, which advocates international fairness and justice, is indeed a strong power in Southern Europe, one of the powerful forces in the Mediterranean. However, at this time of world transformation, succeeding as the leader of the Fascists and 天産 poor, its reserves of coal and iron ore are less than one-fourth of Japan's. Therefore, apart from pioneering in Africa nearby, it is difficult to show off in the world. Therefore, among the five permanent members of the League of Nations, only Britain and France can指揮如意. Their every move is enough to sway the League of Nations. Thereupon, Japan went back and forth between Britain and France, enticing them with market profits and moving them with the defense of 赤化, and thus was able to safely occupy the Northeast. Since the 9/18 Incident of the previous year, our government has adhered to its consistent policy of patience, requesting the League of Nations to promote truth and justice, quietly waiting for the League of Nations to extend its justice to the three northeastern provinces and return the 珠還合浦.

It is unknown that the cunning and sophisticated Japanese imperialists had already obtained the understanding of Britain and France to sweep through the three northeastern provinces and encompass Shanhaiguan. Thereupon, they publicly declared to the world that "Manchuria" had long ceased to belong to our country, and Jehol was also划入 within the scope of Mongolia. Chapter 10 of the Lytton Commission's report also stated that "Japan now enjoys the power in Jehol Province. To be maintained." This clearly recognizes that Jehol belongs to the scope of Manchuria and Mongolia. At least it also expands the rights and interests acquired by Japan's plunder. Japan is not satisfied with this. Furthermore, it does not want to distribute the rights and interests it has acquired through aggression to the powers, and it must have the League of Nations recognize the "Manchuria (puppet) state" manufactured by its military force in order to fulfill its aggressive intentions. As for the true reason why the League of Nations has been slow and slow and procrastinating and procrastinating, it is not that it has any love for our country or that it is doing it for justice. It is actually wanting to obtain some economic benefits in the three northeastern provinces (the "Manchuria (puppet) state" that Japan calls). Japan only verbally expressed that it has no territorial ambitions towards China. The international justice it calls is "the protection of the lifeline." In other words, it is the military occupation of "Manchuria."

㈡ The Incident Has Already Expanded to Within Shanhaiguan

Now, let us cite Foreign Minister Uchida's speech to the House of Peers on January 21 to clarify this. Uchida's statement said:

'...Recognizing the new country and helping its development is to put the Manchurian issue on a solid foundation and resolve it. Furthermore, I am convinced that this is the only way to preserve peace in the East...'

'...In the end, the three countries of Japan, Manchuria, and China are each independent and help each other is the best way to maintain peace in the East...'

'Jehol is a part of "Manchuria," and it is clear from the establishment of various countries. However, recently, it is not only a significant fact that public order is being disrupted in the province, and the regular troops under Zhang Xueliang have also invaded across the border. Maintaining the security of the "Manchukuo" territory is a responsibility jointly borne by the two countries in the Japan-Manchukuo agreement. Therefore, the Jehol issue is purely an internal issue of "Manchukuo." At the same time, it is the thing that our side (Japan) is most concerned about in the treaty obligations...'

'Regarding the invasion of Jehol territory, I have already mentioned that the Empire is deeply concerned about this state of affairs in China and fears that this situation will lead to unfortunate consequences, so I must warn the Chinese government and the Chinese people to pay deep attention in advance. Furthermore, urge them to reflect...'

Uchida's tone not only ignores Sino-Japanese relations, but even lists the puppet state alongside us and puts forward the absurd and absurd "three countries...helping each other." Furthermore, he recognizes that the movement of our troops within our country is "disrupting governance and security." Are the Japanese troops indiscriminately invading our Liaojihei and bombarding Yuguan not 強寇?

At the same time, after reading Foreign Minister Uchida's speech, we should deeply recognize that we must urgently rise up, work hard, and fight to save ourselves.

First. The fall of Yuguan and the situation of苟安 can no longer be幸存. The enemy has gone deep. It is万难to偷惰.

Second. Chaoyang Temple. Beipiao and other places. Has fallen into enemy hands. The Jehol border has also been bombed, and fearing further hidden endurance will leave no room for survival.

Third. For a year and a half, our government fully trusted the League of Nations to maintain peace. The so-called ultimatum that must be answered within 24 hours is nothing more than an empty wish and cannot restrain Japan.

Jehol is now contested by us and coveted by the enemy. If Jehol is unfortunate enough to follow in the footsteps of the northern Manchuria, then Pingjin, as well as Hebei and Shandong, will not be guaranteed. What our people should deeply reflect on at this crisis is nothing more than a struggle of iron and blood. By using iron and blood to resist violent enemies, we can seek a path to life from amidst a hundred deaths.

Duan Qirui Passed Jinan Yesterday and Headed South

(Jinan) This morning at 9:00 AM, Duan Qirui arrived in Jinan on the Pingpu Railway's No. 201 train, in an attached Jingfeng private carriage. Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, and Duan Honggang accompanied him. Qian Yongming, dispatched by Chiang to welcome him in Tianjin, was also on the train. Han Fuju and Zhou Xiuwen, a counselor from the provincial government, greeted him at the station. Duan did not get off the train, but Han boarded to meet and speak with him. Duan praised Han's achievements in governing Shandong. Han invited Duan to stay a little longer when he passed through Jinan on his return north, and Duan agreed. Duan said that people's livelihood is the most important thing, and the North often suffers from drought, so large-scale water conservancy projects are essential. Duan told reporters that his trip to Nanjing was because Mr. Chiang had repeatedly wanted to come north to meet him but had not been able to, and recently sent Mr. Qian to Tianjin to welcome him, expressing that with national difficulties at hand, state affairs should be discussed with national elders, so he could not refuse. Duan said that he could not announce his opinions on state affairs before arriving in Nanjing. Regarding resistance against foreign aggression, material resources are certainly important, but the will and spirit of the people are even more so. It is the critical responsibility of news reporters to promote awareness and awaken the public, and he hoped that they would work hard. Although Duan's hair and beard were white, he was still full of energy, no less than in his younger days. At 9:45 AM, Han and others bid farewell and got off the train. Duan saw them off at the carriage door, nodded in greeting, and continued south on the same train. It is said that Duan plans to stay in Nanjing for three days and in Shanghai for seven days to visit his sister and daughter before returning north. (21st Dispatch)

(Jinan) Duan Qirui told Han Fuju that he often communicated with Chiang Kai-shek and spoke frankly in his letters. Chiang Kai-shek, for various reasons, was unable to implement his suggestions. He also spoke about water conservancy, suggesting that if more reservoirs were built in the upper reaches of the Yellow River, they could reduce flooding downstream during high water and irrigate fields during droughts. He also asked Han which town he was originally from, and Han replied, "Zhanzhen." Duan said that there were people from Zhanzhen's Third Town among his acquaintances and that they had an old relationship. He also said that he had visited the Meng Temple and Mount Tai, but not the Confucius Temple. He added that the fare on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway should be reduced and that the trade union system was also inappropriate. (21st Dispatch)

Hoover and Roosevelt Decide Britain and the U.S. Will Discuss War Debts in Early March

Future Negotiations Will Still Be Difficult

National News Agency, Washington, 20th - After meeting with President-elect Roosevelt today, U.S. President Hoover immediately announced that Britain and the U.S. would discuss the war debt issue in early March. Secretary of State Stimson will arrange all the preparatory procedures, but the actual discussion will be chaired by the new Democratic Secretary of State.

After hearing this news, American political circles generally believe that Davies will be the new Secretary of State in the next term, representing the United States in negotiations with Britain. This is because, among those currently rumored to be the new Secretary of State, only Davies participated in today's important meeting. Today, the two presidents met in the Red Room of the White House. Secretary of State Stimson, Treasury Secretary Mills, Davies, and Roosevelt's economic advisor, Moley, were all present. Afterwards, President Hoover stated that Britain had requested to discuss war debts, and the new government would be happy to receive British representatives in early March. At that time, it would naturally be necessary to discuss world economic issues of mutual concern to Britain and the U.S., and representatives would also be sent to plan methods for advancing the world situation. Hoover's statement on behalf of both the outgoing and incoming governments is seen as clear evidence that the two presidents completely agree on the two major financial issues. The United States has already achieved success in the preparatory committee for the World Economic Conference, removing the war debt issue from its agenda. It is now able to freely discuss the war debt issue on a broader scale. However, if this issue is not resolved, it will still be an obstacle to economic recovery. Therefore, President Hoover is seeking an early resolution based on the recommendations of the preparatory committee. It is now believed that the British war debt issue may be resolved before the opening of the World Economic Conference, which is entirely possible. Upon hearing this news today, American economic circles all considered it constructive good news, and the market prices on the New York Stock Exchange also rose accordingly.

National News Agency, London, 21st - Today, British officials were very satisfied to hear the U.S. President's announcement that they were prepared to discuss the war debt issue with Britain. Britain owes the U.S. a total of $9,818,265,000, accounting for more than half of the total war debts owed to the U.S. by fourteen countries. Britain strongly advocates that, in order to seek to eliminate the shackles of the world economic decline, the entire structure of war debts must be reconsidered, and they especially hope that this matter will be discussed quickly, so that an agreement can be reached before the next payment deadline in mid-June. Although the majority of British people oppose punitive payments, it is expected that a majority in Parliament will oppose making further payments before the matter has been settled. If the negotiations in March do not yield much results, it is feared that the British Cabinet may even be overthrown due to a vote of no confidence. As for Britain's attitude, although it seems to have abandoned the idea of total cancellation, officials have stated that they will not be satisfied with a resolution unless there is a substantial reduction. It is predicted that a satisfactory solution in the future will be selected from one or more of the following items: (1) Reduce the total war debt by 50% or 75%; (2) Cancel the interest, only repaying the principal of the 1923 agreement, totaling 4.6 billion gold yuan, to be repaid in 62 years; (3) Reduce the interest rate from 3.5% to 1%, which is approximately equivalent to reducing the interest by one-third; (4) Agree on a lump sum for complete settlement, with the British government issuing bonds on the American market so that the U.S. government can receive cash, with a maximum amount of 500 million gold yuan. It is now expected that although the U.S. government may allow concessions, it will seek other forms of compensation in exchange, such as preferential tariffs on certain American manufactured goods and duty-free imports of American wheat. However, due to the restrictions of the Ottawa Agreement within Britain, it is feared that there may not be much room for concessions on tariff reductions. It is anticipated that there will be many difficulties in future negotiations, especially regarding the $95 million paid on December 15th of last year, which Britain believes should be included in the final lump sum payment, while the United States believes that the payment should be made on time according to the original agreement, which will be the focus of the dispute.

Japanese Parliament Opens, Saito Announces Policy Direction

Red Menace and Financial Issues Are the Focus of Questions

Japanese Allied News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - The 64th Parliament opened on the 21st. The Prime Minister and other cabinet members arrived at the Diet at 9:30 a.m. The Seiyukai, Minseito, and the opposition National Alliance also attended in full. The audience was already full, and the authorities were on high alert. The House of Peers declared the meeting open at 10:05 a.m. First, Prime Minister Saito delivered a speech on policy direction, followed by Foreign Minister Uchida on foreign policy. Then, Count Niara of the Kenkyukai questioned the Prime Minister, Interior Minister, Army Minister, Navy Minister, and Education Minister on the essence of the national society. The House of Representatives opened at 1:00 p.m. After speeches by the Prime Minister and Foreign Minister, Takahashi, the Minister of Finance, delivered a speech on financial policy. After the Finance Minister finished speaking, Hamada Kokumatsu, a veteran of the Seiyukai, focused on ideological issues and questioned general administrative issues. Then, Oguchi Kiroku began questioning the Finance Minister on the issue of reconstructing emergency finances.

Saito Delivers Speech on Policy Direction

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - Prime Minister Saito's speech in the Diet today outlined the following key points of his policy direction: 1. Manchuria Issue: The Japanese government is pleased to have concluded a protocol with "Manchukuo," taking the lead among other countries in recognizing it and establishing formal diplomatic relations. Since then, the country has been developing towards a sound path, which proves that the government's views are correct. Respecting international faith, cooperating with neighboring countries, maintaining peace in the Far East, and contributing to permanent world peace are the fundamental policies of the Empire's diplomacy. The government will provide appropriate assistance to "Manchukuo" during its establishment, and it is deeply believed that this is the most urgent task at that time. 2. Budget Issue: The total amount of the Showa 8th year budget is 2.239 billion yuan, which is an unavoidable expenditure in the current situation. As a result, the revenue is 895 million yuan short, and it is inevitable to resort to public bonds. Some may fear for the future of the finances, but the financial community has improved once, and it is hoped that the revenue will increase. In terms of expenditure, expenses such as the Manchurian Incident and the improvement of military equipment will not require as much funding as they do now. Once the balance of payments is restored, I believe that the finances will be greatly improved in a few years. 3. Ideological Issue: It is a pity that there are recently dangerous ideas that are incompatible with the national essence. However, it is also a pity that there are reactionary individuals who want to take violent direct action. The government will not only crack down on them, but also actively guide thoughts through political education. 4. Situation Recovery Issue: The recovery of rural villages and small and medium-sized businesses and industries is currently underway. The result has been a decline in exchange rates, which has promoted exports. Small and medium-sized businesses and industries have therefore seen a major turnaround. At the same time, the government has launched a national regeneration movement, hoping to open up the difficult situation with the unity of the entire country. 5. Trade Improvement Issue: Foreign trade has greatly improved, and the industrial community has shown signs of activity. The signs of economic recovery are already very obvious. However, the government is further seeking to assist important industries. 6. Political Purification Issue: The current cabinet takes the purification of politics as one of its missions. Therefore, it plans to submit an amendment to the election law to this session of the Diet. 7. Conclusion: In short, the situation in diplomacy and domestic affairs has not yet escaped the realm of emergency. The Empire will thoroughly believe in its beliefs, devote all its efforts to establishing international justice and contributing to world peace, and internally promote the national spirit in order to open up the difficult situation.

Takahashi Delivers Speech on Financial Situation

Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - The House of Representatives opened this meeting at 1:00 p.m. Prime Minister Saito and Foreign Minister Uchida's speeches were the same as those delivered in the House of Peers. Later, Takahashi, the Minister of Finance, at the high age of 80, took the stage to deliver a speech on finances as follows: The expenditures for the Showa 8th year are nearly 2.239 billion, so they cannot all be covered by ordinary revenue. Today, the plans for increasing taxes and other revenues seem to be gradually recovering from the economic situation, so everything is handled by public bonds. The recent situation in the general economic community, even in countries around the world, is still in a sad state, so its future is difficult to predict. However, Japan is different from Europe and the United States. There is no difficulty in compensating for war debts, and the foreign debt is not huge, and it is in a position of science. Since the ban on gold, the foreign exchange rate has fallen, and the reason is the actual situation of international payments. The main concern is the international instability centered on the Manchurian issue and inflation, and the result is to encourage natural exports and open up new sales channels. If the exchange rate falls too low, there will be disadvantages, so the Exchange Control Law is proposed at this meeting to further prevent investment methods. Also, in terms of finances, the issuance of huge amounts of public bonds will inevitably lead to an increase in currency issuance, so it is impossible not to worry about the undesirable results. However, for the purpose of so-called reasonable control of currency, the Bank of Japan prevents the disadvantages of inflation, so there are no disadvantages.

House of Representatives Questions Red Menace Issue

Japanese Allied News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - The House of Representatives opened at 1:15 p.m. After the speech by Finance Minister Takahashi, Seiyukai member Hamada Kokumatsu led the questioning. Hamada took the stage, first analyzing the so-called extraordinary era, advising on the abnormal current situation of the political organization, and referring to the national ideology issue, saying that judicial officials internally produced Communist Party members, and that communism gradually infiltrated the military. How does the government deal with these communist elements? Hamada then questioned the government's beliefs regarding recent diplomatic issues, and also brought up the issue of the Bank of Japan's urgent sale of public bonds and the issue of inflation from December 14th to January 14th of last year, condemning the government's negligence. The debate lasted for an hour and a half before he left the stage. Prime Minister Saito responded that the satisfactory development of constitutional government is what he desires, so he will spare no effort in the progress of political parties. The communist party incident will be handled with all efforts. The truth of the May 15th Incident has not yet reached the time to be announced. Justice Minister Koyama then took the stage to reply that the May 15th Incident cannot be announced at this time. Hamaguchi continued to press the Prime Minister on this issue, but the Prime Minister did not answer, and Hamaguchi had no choice but to stop questioning. Oguchi Kiroku of the Seiyukai took the stage in turn and began questioning. Oguchi stated that he did not oppose the issuance of huge amounts of public bonds, but that the government's handling methods for the finances of the ninth year, the tenth year, and the future. How will the expenses for the improvement of military equipment, the foreign exchange loss, and the emergency recovery affect the future financial plan? What is the Finance Minister's determination regarding the administrative and financial reorganization investigation committee? Oguchi also turned to questioning general economic issues, asking what level the government believes is most appropriate for commodity prices and currency circulation, and why the Finance Minister did not prevent the urgent and rapid decline of the exchange rate. If the exchange rate presents an unnatural surge in the future, what measures will the government take? Finance Minister Takahashi replied, explaining the reasons why he could not determine the future financial plan in the current situation, and also revealing the government's beliefs on this. Then, Kawasaki Katsu of the Minseito took the stage to question, stating that the budget for the eighth year relies heavily on public bonds, and the result is that the financial faction is weakened, and it causes the exchange rate to plummet. The increase in public bonds is a permanent burden, and the low-price policy has no great benefits. Those who benefit from protective tariffs and the fall of the exchange rate should naturally have the obligation to bear and relieve this national loss. In order to stabilize the exchange rate, there is no other method than to improve international lending, establish a financial foundation, and restore domestic credit. Inflation caused by the fall in the exchange rate is a major threat to the lives of the common people. What rescue measures does the government have for this? Minister of Commerce Takahashi took the stage to reply, stating that the government's budget expansion and public bond policy were by no means without a plan. The reason for the fall in the exchange rate is inappropriate for the argument that the income and expenditure are unbalanced. After the Finance Minister replied, Prime Minister Saito stated that he had no need to reply. Then Kawasaki and the Finance Minister questioned each other on the issue of increasing taxes, and the meeting adjourned at 6:49 p.m.

Future of Manchurian Plan Unpredictable

China United News Agency, Tokyo, 21st - After Finance Minister Takahashi's speech in the Lower House today, Seiyukai financier Oguchi Kiroku criticized Takahashi, saying that the government's budget was short by about 90 million yuan, which was very unreasonable to fully cover with public bonds. The government must fundamentally solve the Manchurian Incident and the financial resources for emergency relief. Takahashi replied that the future of the Manchurian plan is still chaotic, the international political situation is still dangerous, and it may be resolved in five or ten years, but it is difficult to predict at present. Therefore, the necessary expenses in the future are still unknown. The financial problem is in this state, and it cannot be fundamentally solved. It can be seen that the future of Japan's finances has been unable to make up for the military expenses of the invasion.

A Glimpse of the Japanese Army's Oppression of the People in Northeast China

Fabricating False News to Incite People's Hearts

Forcing Celebrations for the New Year to Falsely Embellish Peace

Ordering the Puppet Army to Attack Jehol to Make Us Harm Each Other

Changchun Correspondence, the people here are most concerned about the fighting at Yuguan, and they spare no effort to search for real news in order to know the progress of our military in Guannei. Japan, fearing the worries of the rear and the people uniting to resist, fabricated all kinds of news unfavorable to us, forced local newspapers to publish it, and broadcast it to the people. Therefore, since the outbreak of the Yuguan war, there has been no news here that is favorable to us. At the same time, Japan fabricated unfounded news such as Zhang Xueliang's escape, the collapse of the Northeast Army, and the Shanxi army entering Tianjin and Beijing to seize territory. Upper-level people can identify the truth and falsehood of the news, but lower-level people mistakenly believe it to be true. Therefore, those who clench their fists and grieve in secret are unknown. Newspapers must pay the highest price to publish the news from the puppet state news agency, and deleting and altering it is not allowed. When publishing, the title should also clearly show that the Chinese are the enemy, otherwise it is not allowed to be published. No newspaper dares to disobey. Some merchants or wealthier households secretly install radio receivers in their homes and secretly listen to the Beijing and Ping radio broadcasts every night, relying on them as the only source of real hope. However, the radio broadcasts often exaggerate and are not factual, so the people dare not fully believe them. Those who come from Guannei are asked if there is any news. Once something is heard, people, whether they know each other or not, spread the word around as a mutual comfort. The taste of being slaves of a subjugated nation has been fully experienced by the 30 million people in Northeast China for a year. Recently, the Japanese have also restricted the installation of radio receivers, probably wanting to completely cut off the hope of the Chinese.

Recently, because the Lunar New Year is approaching, Japan is anesthetizing the Chinese people and embellishing peace. The main Japanese agencies in various places distribute Spring Festival couplets and gods, such as Heaven, Earth, Emperor, and 君, and give multiple copies to each agency, group, and store, forcing them to be posted in a timely manner. They also ordered the puppet state propaganda committees in the major ports of Jilin, Liaoning, Changchun, Harbin, and Heilongjiang to prepare Lunar New Year celebration parties, hold dragon lantern stilt walking and other lower-level acrobatics, and lure the Chinese people into forgetting their country and their worries. However, groups and stores in this environment and as slaves of a subjugated nation have no such interest. Remembering that during the Gregorian New Year, Japan tried its best to pressure merchants and groups to send congratulatory letters, but the merchants were fundamentally lacking in interest and did not tacitly agree. Except for people in the agencies, no one was willing to send letters to congratulate the New Year. Therefore, for the Lunar New Year, the Japanese will order the responsible groups to urge them to celebrate the New Year with all their strength. After the subjugation of the Northeast, the people's thoughts and spirits are also not allowed to be free. The Japanese army is invading Jehol and plans to form five mixed brigades of the puppet state army. Each brigade has four regiments, three brigades are recruited by Jilin and Liaoning, and two brigades are recruited by Heilongjiang. The Japanese will allocate military equipment and bullets and order them to go to the Jehol border within a month or so, wanting to first make our compatriots harm each other, and then the Japanese army will take advantage of our exhaustion to attack forward. Recently, due to insufficient recruitment, it is planned to order the two brigades of Shen Cheng of the pseudo-suppression bandit army in Jilin and the two detachments of Zhou Zuolin and Wang Kezhen of the pseudo-Heilongjiang army to be organized into mixed brigades and dispatched to Jehol in the shortest possible time. However, Zhou and Wang still have some conscience and are still hesitant about harming their own flesh and blood. They are still unwilling to reorganize. The Japanese army is eager to attack Jehol and may seek other pseudo-armies in the future. (January 11)

Recent Situation After the Fall of Yuguan

Sparse Population Within Thirty Miles of the War Zone

The Morale East of the Luan River Is Very High

Changli Correspondence, residents within thirty miles south of Qinhuangdao and east, west of Shanhaiguan, north of Shimen Village and east, and west of Jiumenkou, who have the ability to evacuate, have long evacuated elsewhere. Because the area has become a major war zone, not only is the population sparse, but even pigs, sheep, and poultry are rarely left behind. The desolate scene can be described. As for the recent situation in the war zone, it is briefly described as follows:

Neutral Zone Delineated Within Our Territory

Because of the Sino-British joint venture in the Kailuan Coal Mine in Qinhuangdao, the Kailuan Coal Mine Wharf was built along the coast south of the railway. The British section chief of the Qinhuangdao station of the Beining Railway, Ceylon, and two British naval captains vigorously mediated and designated the area south of the railway as a neutral zone. No Chinese soldiers in military uniforms were allowed to cross south of the railway, and no Japanese soldiers in leather hats and leather clothes were allowed to cross the line. It is a painful matter of humiliating compromise to delineate a Chinese-Japanese buffer neutral zone within Chinese territory. However, since our soldiers regard this railway as a gulf, the residents have also moved from north of the railway to south of the railway in succession, thinking it is a place to avoid disaster.

Enemy Marines Land to Demonstrate

At around 4:00 a.m. this morning (16th), more than 20 marines from the Japanese warship in Qinhuangdao suddenly landed from the Kailuan Wharf and armed themselves to break into the so-called neutral zone south of the railway to demonstrate and provoke. The situation suddenly became tense. Our army immediately made proper preparations. Many residents south of the railway were awakened from their sleep, not knowing where to go, or were panicked. But before long, the Japanese soldiers retreated, and the situation also temporarily eased. However, no matter how local the easing is, it is ultimately difficult to break the Japanese warlords' predetermined plan of aggression against us.

The Great Yuguan慰勞团 on the Front Trenches

The Scene in Changli County Is Desolate

Changli County, ninety miles west of Qinhuangdao, closes its city gates every night at 8:00 p.m. The families of all the officers have already moved to Tianjin and Beijing. The wealthy people in the area are also preparing to evacuate. Major commercial factories such as the Xinhua Cannery have already stopped working. Schools and groups such as Huimin Middle School have also taken early vacations. But the people east of the Luan River, although in the terror of the war, deeply hope that they can win in one battle and defeat the enemy for the sake of the nation. Destroying their homes to relieve the country's difficulties is also without complaint. The morale is so high.

Xu Yaowu, a Wounded Soldier of the Ninth Brigade Defending Yuguan

Yuguan Traitors Sell Out the Country for Glory

After the fall of Shanhaiguan, traitors appeared one after another. The most famous are: (1) Na Qifu, the former director of the Beining Railway Bridge Factory, which is located in Shanhaiguan. It is our country's only railway bridge factory. The machines in the factory are worth more than 9 million taels. After Shanhaiguan fell, Na immediately surrendered to the Japanese army, requested to maintain his original position, and filled out a surrender application to the Japanese Kwantung Army's Ichii Valley, still serving as the director of the factory. On the 10th, he immediately gathered the workers and started work as usual. From then on, our country's railway construction bridge engineering will have to borrow from foreigners. (2) Ma Hongru, who participated in the Tianjin Incident, was once wanted by the authorities. After that, he served as the director of the Yuguan Branch of the Special Public Security Bureau of Hebei Province, whose authority was above the county magistrate. During the Yuguan Incident, Ma led his staff to the west gate of the city and took the stage to give a shameless speech to the evacuees, saying, "You don't have to evacuate, even if you evacuate to Tianjin and Beijing, you still have to return to Japan." On the one hand, he blocked the people from leaving the city, and his crimes are too numerous to count. He has now been promoted by the Japanese army to the director of the Shanhaiguan Police Bureau. (3) Li Detong, the former stationmaster of the Shanhaiguan Station of the Beining Railway, had an important position and a generous salary. After our army retreated, he was appointed by the puppet government to continue his original post and urged the employees to maintain the traffic of the pseudo-Fengshan Road. (4) Director Sun of the Beining Railway Shanhaiguan Hospital (name unknown) has also surrendered to the enemy and led his subordinates to run the Japanese wounded soldiers hospital, which is a life-saving machine for treating the enemy. The equipment of the Beining Railway Hospital is the best among the railway hospitals in the country. Now that it is used to help the enemy, is it enough for the traitor's flesh to be eaten? (January 18)

Establishment of the Guangdong Provincial Air Defense Committee

Raising Funds for the Defense of Airspace

Air Defense Equipment to be Designed by Experts

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, due to the urgency of the national crisis, the province of Guangdong is reorganizing national defense, and the public is also rising to assist. Representatives from all sectors of Guangzhou convened a conference on solidifying air defense at the provincial party headquarters on the 13th of this month. Over a hundred representatives from various sectors attended, and it was immediately decided to organize an air defense committee, with the Anti-Japanese Federation of Municipal Schools, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Silver Trade Association, the Machine Workers' Union, the Eastern Suburb Farmers' Association, the Lawyers' Association, the National Salvation Association, the Women's Federation, the Overseas Comrades' Association, the Teahouse Workers' Union, and the Civil University Student Autonomous Association, eleven groups in total, as members of the air defense committee. A method for raising air defense funds was also decided upon. On the 16th, the air defense committee was formally established, and the executive committee members were sworn into office. The National Salvation Association, the Anti-Japanese Federation of Municipal Schools, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Teahouse Workers' Union, and the Women's Federation were designated as standing committee members. The Silver Trade Union, the Machine Workers' Union, the Overseas Comrades' Association, the Civil University Student Association, and the Lawyers' Association were designated as members of the custodial committee. The provincial party headquarters was designated as the director of the general affairs section, the Anti-Japanese Federation of Municipal Schools as the director of the propaganda section, and the Municipal Senior High School Association as the director of the finance section. The office address is temporarily located at the organizational section of the provincial party headquarters. The committee's regular expenses are 950 yuan per month, to be allocated monthly by the provincial government upon a letter from the provincial party headquarters. The task of the air defense committee is to prepare funds to be used for the defense of the city's airspace in the event of an international war. The funds raised will be properly managed by the committee and must not be used for other purposes. The methods for raising air defense funds include five items: (1) Selling sealed enemy goods, allocating 50% of the proceeds; (2) Allocating 20% of the prize money from charitable lotteries, and allocating all unclaimed prize money, with a three-month limit; (3) Collecting half a month's rent from all shops and houses in the city, to be borne by the landlords; (4) Voluntary donations; (5) Other funds raised are to be exclusively used for air defense. Collection of charitable lottery prize money was set to begin on the 16th. Collection of shop and house rent will be entrusted to the Public Security Bureau from February 1st. It is reported that the air defense committee has hired experts to design air defense equipment, with a total cost of under 10 million yuan. In addition to the 1 million yuan each allocated by the provincial and municipal governments, the air defense committee can also raise over 1 million yuan. Additional needed funds will be raised through donations from wealthy individuals. (January 17th)

Wuxi

A Bird's-Eye View of the Silk Industry in Jiangsu and Zhejiang

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry, after a decision by the provincial government, is being abolished, and its affiliated agencies have also been ordered to close down, effective at the end of last year, to be directly received and managed by the respective county governments. Although the silk industry circles of various counties have been running around and appealing, they have failed to persuade the authorities to reverse their decision. After receiving the order, the county government appointed Shen Xichun as the custodian of the county farm and Wen Yiqing as the assistant. They arrived at the farm on the 1st of this month to take over, which was handed over by the acting director Hua Qian. As for planting work, it is still proceeding as usual to avoid neglect and damage, which has been reported to the county magistrate Chen for review and approval. However, the county's farm is a production agency, and its closure will greatly damage agriculture. Therefore, local people, recognizing this, are actively planning remedial measures to avoid interruption. Moreover, the silk industry in the county is unusually developed, leading all other counties, with annual production of several million yuan. In the heyday of silk factories, there were as many as fifty-five in urban and rural areas. In the previous years, due to the disastrous defeat in the silk market, the capital of the factories was almost entirely depleted, and they closed down one after another. The number of unemployed workers reached forty or fifty thousand. Last autumn, the silk market showed signs of recovery, and the factories resumed operation one after another, with more than twenty factories in operation, which was able to temporarily maintain the status quo. It was hoped that the silk market would recover this year, so as to make up for the losses. Therefore, attention must be paid to the selection of seeds, silkworm rearing, and silk reeling, and it is hoped that the government will provide guidance and assistance. Unexpectedly, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Industry suddenly announced its abolition, and silk cocoon merchants were left without leadership, causing widespread panic. At this time, the authorities in Zhejiang Province felt the need to promote and improve the silk industry. Because the province lacked silkworm seeds, it could not promote and improve the industry, so it purchased a large number of silkworm seeds from Jiangsu Province, preparing to actively promote the industry. When the leaders of the silk industry in Wuxi heard this news, they were extremely panicked, because the original local species in Wuxi had long been eliminated, and it all depended on the cultivation of improved seeds. Now that the silkworm seeds have been suddenly taken away by Zhejiang Province, the silk industry in Wuxi will inevitably suffer a setback and cannot be saved. In order to remedy this, it is planned to set up a silkworm breeding center and purchase 10,000 silkworm egg sheets for use. The required funds will be raised by borrowing, and it can be implemented as soon as it is settled, so as to avoid the silk industry and the farmers' economy from falling into a desperate situation.

Changzhou

Coffin Robbery Occurs in Xujia Bridge

Ye, the deceased mother of Xu Zhenzhi, the head of Gudian Township in the eighteenth district of Wujin County, passed away in the city residence some time ago. The coffin was kept at home. When the Shanghai war broke out, a boat was hired to transport the coffin back to the hometown and placed next to Xujia Bridge. It was scheduled to be buried with her deceased husband on the 26th of this month according to the lunar calendar. Unexpectedly, the coffin was stolen by bandits the night before last. A corner of the coffin lid was cut off, all the burial objects were looted, and the corpse was damaged, which was too horrible to describe. After the incident, it was reported to the nearby Public Security Fourth Branch for investigation. Yesterday (the 20th), district head Zhu Yizheng also reported to the county government for arrest.

Nantong

Police Officer Executed for Stopping Car and Committing Murder

Sun Ruhe, a squad leader of the tax police, and Xu Jiaming, a police officer, set up a roadblock at the Tangzha River estuary. When they failed to stop a car, they fired three shots, hitting Gu Yinglong, the principal of Baipu School, in the back of the head, killing him instantly. The criminal police officers then forced the driver to take the corpse to Rugao. Road police stopped them for inspection. Sun Ruhe falsely accused the deceased of being a salt smuggler and claimed to take him to the headquarters for investigation. When the car arrived at Baipu, it was intercepted by the police and regiment and sent to the court. On the 20th, magistrate Sheng interrogated them. Sun Ruhe confessed to stopping the car and firing the shots. Xu Jiaming confessed to stopping the car. The driver, Qian Er, and other passengers, Li Rongqing, testified. After the debate, the court announced the verdict on the spot. Sun Ruhe was sentenced to death for intentional homicide. Xu Jiaming was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for obstructing freedom.

Yangzhou

Since the Japanese army repeatedly invaded the city of Yangzhou, the financial situation has been indirectly affected quite a bit. Pinghu

Boat Robbed En Route on Jiaoshi Route

The express boat traveling between Pinghu and Jiaoshi was robbed the other day when it reached a place six miles from Jiaoshi. Suddenly, two passengers ordered the boat to stop ashore. As soon as the mooring cable was tied, two people with short guns were seen on the shore. They, along with the two passengers, broke into the cabin and searched it thoroughly. Ningbo

Mother and Daughter Commit Suicide Due to Marriage Issues

Wang Guixiang, a resident of Dongwu in Yinxian County, is engaged in farming and his family is well-off. His wife, surnamed Mou, is over forty years old and has a daughter who is now nineteen years old and has a beautiful face. In September of this year, her mother arranged for her to marry the third son of Zhang Baosheng in the same village. However, Wang's daughter was deeply unwilling, so after being betrothed to the Zhang family, she became depressed. When Mr. and Mrs. Wang saw their daughter so dejected, they also had regrets. A few days ago, they begged the original matchmaker to break off the engagement with the Zhang family, willing to return the engagement gift of 110 yuan. The Zhang family agreed to dissolve the engagement, as the daughter was unwilling and could not be forced. Originally, nothing further should have occurred, but Zhang Baosheng's eldest son made excessive demands, saying that it would cost no less than 300 yuan. Mr. Wang's family was not wealthy enough to comply immediately, which caused friction within the family. Unexpectedly, Wang's wife, feeling wronged by her husband and daughter, was filled with remorse and committed suicide by swallowing opium on the morning of the day before yesterday (the 17th). By the time her family discovered it, she had already died from the poison. Wang's daughter, grieving over her mother's tragic death and believing herself to be responsible, also committed suicide with scissors on the morning of the next day (the 18th). Wang Guixiang was deeply saddened by the tragic changes in his family and took a boat to Ningbo that afternoon, complaining to the Yinxian County Local Court that his wife and daughter's deaths were caused by the coercion of Zhang Baosheng's eldest son, requesting the arrest of the perpetrator and legal action. After receiving the report, the court immediately sent prosecutor Fang to examine the bodies and investigate the truth of the case.

Jiaxing

Appealing Criminal Jumps off Train to Escape

Yao Jinguan from the Xinxin District of Jiaxing was sentenced by the Jiaxing Local Branch Court to five years of imprisonment for helping to hide Yang A'er, who had seduced Lu San'nan, a girl under the age of twenty. Yang A'er was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. Yang and Yao appealed because they were not satisfied with the verdict. After the High Court held a hearing, it rejected the appeal. On the 20th, the two criminals were handed over to Zhao Ruilin, a patrol captain, and Luo Rong, a police officer, of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, who took them to Jiaxing by train. When the train passed Wangdian Station, Yao Jinguan claimed that he needed to urinate and asked to have his handcuffs released. The patrol captain released them. Unexpectedly, Yao jumped off the train after entering the toilet and escaped. Zhao immediately jumped off the train to chase after leaving the files and Yang in the care of the police. After the train arrived at the station, the police escorted Yang to the branch court, but it was not accepted because the criminals were not all there. Later, the police escorted the criminal to the Public Security Bureau, which kept both the police officer and the criminal under custody while informing the Wangdian Public Security Branch Bureau to investigate and arrest the fugitive.

Local News

Sun Ke Discusses the Political Participation Council and the Draft Constitution

Formulating Laws and Regulations for Autumn Convocation

Completing the Constitution in One Year at the Earliest

The League of Nations is Powerless; Only Self-Reliance Can Save Us

Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, accompanied by Liang Hancao, Secretary-General of the Legislative Yuan, and members of the Legislative Yuan, Ma Chaojun, Jian Youwen, Chen Jianru, Zhong Tianxin, and others, arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing on the night before last. Yesterday, a reporter from this newspaper interviewed Mr. Sun. According to Mr. Sun, the Political Participation Council is expected to be convened this autumn, and the draft constitution can be completed in one year at the earliest. A detailed record of his remarks is as follows:

Convocation of the Political Participation Council

Mr. Sun first stated that the convocation of the Political Participation Council had been stipulated by the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee to be convened within this year. The original proposal was transferred to the Central Standing Committee, and then to the Central Political Council, to determine the principles of the organizational law of the Political Participation Council. Then, the Legislative Yuan would draft laws and regulations based on the principles. However, the Central Political Council has recently been busy discussing other important issues, so the principles of the organizational law of the council have not yet been discussed. It is expected that all laws and regulations can be formulated and officially convened this autumn.

Drafting of the Constitution

Mr. Sun continued, regarding the drafting of the constitution, the Legislative Yuan has organized a Constitution Drafting Committee with more than 30 members. For the sake of special caution, it was decided to widely solicit opinions from all parties, first dividing into several groups, each focusing on a specific issue for thorough discussion. The results of each group's research will be reported to the committee, which will decide on a principle and send it to the Central Political Council for review. After it is passed, the Constitution Committee will draft the initial draft of the constitution, and then hire domestic experts to solicit opinions on the initial draft, so as to conduct public research in order to gather wisdom. Then, gather opinions from all parties, revise it again, and form a perfect constitution, so that when it is implemented in the future, there will be no difficulties. Therefore, the completion of the constitution will take at least one year.

Revision of Civil and Criminal Law

In addition, regarding the current civil law, because there is no interpretation, it is planned to formulate interpretations of civil law, so that law enforcers know the central legislative intent. The current criminal law is mostly based on the drafts from the Beijing government era, which are largely unsuitable and should be revised. The land law still needs to continue to promulgate the land implementation law. The autonomy law has too many ideals, resulting in inconvenience in internal implementation, all of which must be reformed and reorganized. The labor and commercial laws are only partial and must also be completed. In short, there is much criticism from the outside world about the current laws. The reason is that they focus too much on theory and not enough on practice, resulting in a failure to conform to the Chinese situation. All of this must be revised in the future. At the same time, because the issue of law is a specialized subject, slight carelessness is enough to lead to many omissions, so meticulous research is essential.

National Salvation Through Self-Reliance

The League of Nations' handling of the Sino-Japanese incident has shown that it is powerless. The only effect of the just voice of our country's representatives in the international community is to win the sympathy of world opinion. Our country can only resolve to resist Japan to the end, taking strength as the premise. Use as much strength as you have. Cooperate from top to bottom and resist to the end. The generals in North China also have the greatest determination to resist for self-defense, without being discouraged or intimidated. National salvation can only be achieved through self-reliance.

Duan Qirui Goes South

Mr. Sun then talked about the situation in North China, saying that although Duan Qirui's ideas are relatively old, he loves the country and can guarantee that he will not lag behind others. Now that he has resolutely gone south, we naturally express our great welcome. From now on, all unfounded rumors can be dispelled, and Duan himself will not be exploited by villains. As for Director Wang, he is currently recuperating at a spa hospital in the Czech Republic and will be able to return home in about two or three weeks.

Meeting at the Cultural Center

As for my trip to Shanghai, it is to attend the preparatory meeting of the Zhongshan Cultural Education Center tomorrow (i.e., today). This is a weekly routine meeting. Because preparations are just beginning, I have to attend in person. I plan to go to Nanjing in a day or two to actively carry out the work of the Legislative Yuan.

Letter from the Association to Abolish War to Zhang Qun

Offering Methods for Reorganizing the Sichuan Situation

The League to Abolish Internal War sent a letter to Zhang Qun, chairman of the Sichuan Affairs Reorganization Committee, yesterday: "Mr. Yuejun, the Sichuan war dispute is urgently awaiting settlement. Our association, based on its war aspiration to abolish internal war, previously publicly elected representatives to petition the Third Plenary Session of the Central Committee to resolutely stop it. On the 11th of November, we invited academic and commercial groups from Sichuan in Shanghai to jointly discuss and resolve five measures to telegraph to the central government to adopt. The second of those measures was to request the central government to quickly organize the Sichuan Affairs Reorganization Committee, with you as the chairman, with senior central officials and representatives of the people from the war industry inside and outside Sichuan as members, and no active military personnel to participate. Recently, reading the newspaper, I learned that the central government has adopted the association's suggestion to organize the Reorganization Committee and appointed you to preside over it. Upon hearing the news, we were exceedingly delighted. You were formerly the mayor of Shanghai and your governance achievements were obvious. Now reorganizing the Sichuan situation, you will certainly uphold the long-cherished aspiration of peace and comprehensiveness, and set a plan for long-term security, so that the Sichuan generals will be moved by your sincere love for the country, the hometown, and the people, and will readily accept and implement it step by step. Will this not benefit the people of Sichuan and change the international outlook? Now, the five measures resolved by our association are enclosed for your perusal. May they be used as reference. Not presuming to hope too much. I wish you well." Attached is a copy of the five urgent measures to stop the Sichuan war: "(1) Request the central government to order the Sichuan army to cease fire immediately. (2) Request the central government to quickly organize the Sichuan Affairs Reorganization Committee, with Zhang Qun as the chairman, with senior central officials and representatives of the professional people inside and outside Sichuan as members, and no active military personnel to participate. (3) Request the central government to authorize the Reorganization Committee with full authority to reorganize the Sichuan army, transfer them to recover lost territories, and perform the duties of suppressing bandits and guarding the border. At the same time, reorganize the people's wealth, group parties, and other administrations, and let the people's militia take charge of public security throughout the province, and prepare to convene a provincial people's congress to discuss long-term peace and security measures. (4) Request the central government to strictly prohibit the entry of arms and ammunition into Sichuan. (5) Request the central government to investigate and deal with the culprits of the Sichuan war and issue a clear order in advance that those who do not obey the Reorganization Committee's orders will be severely punished without leniency."

Reasons for Silk Factory Shutdown

Sharp Drop in Japanese Silk Prices

Approaching Lunar New Year

There are a total of 113 single and double palace silk factories in the city. Because the sales of European and American silk have been declining year after year, the silk factories have been unable to support themselves and have closed down one after another. In the summer months of June and July last year, only a dozen silk factories in the city were barely able to operate. Later, the government encouraged exports, exempted the old silk factories from export tax and special tax, and issued silk public bonds, with a subsidy of 100 taels of silver per package. As a result, the silk factories resumed operation one after another, reeling old cocoons. For a time, the number of silk factories that resumed operation reached 65. The sales of European and American silk once turned smooth. However, because Japanese silk resumed low-price competition in overseas markets, the sales of Chinese silk in Europe remained sluggish. In addition, at the end of last year, a well-known silk company in New York declared bankruptcy, and the sales of European and American silk universally became cheap, especially Japanese silk. The price of Yokohama Japanese silk fell sharply by 140 to 150 yen, even breaking the standard of 800 yen. Current silk is only opened at 775 yen. As a result, the Shanghai silk market has become even more lifeless. After the New Year, the silk factories have closed down one after another. In addition, the Lunar New Year is approaching, and the customs of the female workers are difficult to change. They all need to take a holiday. Therefore, the number of silk factories that have stopped work has reached eight or nine out of ten. As of yesterday, there are only four or five silk factories in Shanghai that are still finishing their work. They will all stop work and take a holiday tomorrow.

Bean and Rice Industry to Switch to New Weights and Measures

Implementation from January 30th

The Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Association notified all members yesterday that they would switch to new weights and measures: "We hereby inform you that the measuring instruments used by our members have been modified according to the styles promulgated by the government and have been inspected by the Municipal Social Bureau and the Metrology Inspection Institute, which verified their accuracy. Each instrument has been stamped for identification. The weighing instruments used have also been purchased new from the Inspection Institute by our members. We have reported to the Municipal Social Bureau and have been approved to switch to the new measuring instruments and weighing instruments in the north and south markets from January 30th of this year. Except for the scales, which will be changed to the new system at the same time as the Jianghai Customs due to foreign trade relations, all old measuring instruments and weighing instruments used in the past will be abolished. This is to notify all parties, and if the old measuring instruments and weighing instruments are still used, or those that have not been inspected and stamped, they will be punished according to law once they are found. Please do not delay or mistake yourself. This is to notify all."
