Movie Special

Movies and Literary Tastes

— Huang Zhenxia

The following are just some personal feelings obtained in the movie theater. Each paragraph is written as an essay, because it is not serious criticism, so it does not consider the limitations of time or other types of critical articles. It does not write about every movie. I only record the ones I thought were good or touched me. Everything is very free, but responsible.

㈠ The Last Squadron

A portrayal of an ancient battlefield, the crystallization of comradeship, the power of resistance reaching the breaking point.

The whole film is heavily Germanized, but this Germanization is not modern, but ancient, historical. All the cleanliness, order, and scientificization that modern Germans pay attention to are not seen in the film. However, its vigorous and resolute spirit, as well as the unique sorrow and discipline of the Nordic people, are constantly trying to be expressed. The era of the story is 1806, when Napoleon's army was sweeping through Prussia. In the history of the 19th century, we have read how the Prussian territory was hopelessly destroyed in the Battle of Jena, just like our Northeast before and after the September 18th Incident. This story vividly narrates the era that the Germans considered a great disgrace, and the crystallization of the whole film is the epic of a Prussian non-commissioned officer and his twelve soldiers who fought to the death after the disastrous defeat at Jena. It also includes some very temporary soft emotions caused by the village girl Dora, as well as the tragic experience of comrades loving each other from life to death.

In short, the significance of this film is to reveal the military's obedience and death. There is no great principle of the nation or the public. Everything is discipline, the power of discipline, discipline to the death! Therefore, the highest character in the film is a captain (squadron leader), but when they come into contact, the number of people in the company has long been reduced to the smallest unit of the battle, the squad (twelve people). In the end, only the French general is seen taking off his hat and solemnly paying his military salute to the bloody and blurred enemy corpses, while the sound waves mourning the dead slowly rise, and the curtain falls.

A scene from the Laurel and Hardy feature film "Pack Up Your Troubles."

Audience Opinions

Review of "Don't Waste Tonight"

— Jiang Qing

"Don't Waste Tonight" premiered at the Cathay Theatre.

The content and plot of this film are roughly about a singer pursuing the man she admires, initially being rejected, and later succeeding. Therefore, the characteristics of the whole play are characterized by fierce expressions and lively plots, which can be called a romantic comedy.

The protagonist is Swanson, who is known for her flirtatiousness. Her performance can be said to have reached perfection, but her movements are a bit excessive. There are several places in the plot that are not very good, and seem to be inconsistent with common sense. The director's skills are very good, and the light and angle of the photography are particularly exquisite, making people feel very beautified. The several supporting actors are also very good, so they can complement each other.

In short, this film is well worth seeing.

Review of "Dragon Soaring, Phoenix Dancing"

— Jingwu

"Dragon Soaring, Phoenix Dancing," known as the first shot of Wufa's bombardment, finally met us at the Nanjing Grand Theatre the day before yesterday.

The story of "Dragon Soaring, Phoenix Dancing" takes place in 1814, when Napoleon failed and was exiled to Elba Island. All the kings and politicians in Europe were happily celebrating in Vienna. At this time, Tsar Alexander of Russia met the local beauty Crystal. At the first so-called "Conference Dance", just as everyone was having fun, it was suddenly reported that Napoleon had landed in France. Everyone hurriedly dispersed, and a dream of joy turned into a bubble.

The story is very ordinary, but technically speaking, this film is indeed a successful work. Lilian Harvey played Crystal, and her performance was lively and lovely. How touching was the song she sang when she went to the Russian Emperor's new residence and in the carriage! She is truly worthy of being the European Empress of Shadows. Henry Garat played Tsar Alexander of Russia, and his performance was romantic and satisfying. Rirdankova's noble woman, and the scene of the fake emperor flirting with her, was really excellent. The other supporting actors were also able to perform their duties well. The lighting was very suitable, and the Bai language was also fluent. The jokes and interpolations were all satisfying, but at the Conference Dance, the scene where the Russian Emperor and Crystal danced was too long and complicated. The rest was very good.

In short, this film can indeed be called a "masterpiece" on Wufa.

"Dragon Soaring, Phoenix Dancing"

— Yin

(Omitted above) The director of the film is very smart, and the clock selection is also flexible and moving. For example, the clock when the Austrian Prince Metternich read out the resolution after the end of the conference was expressed very deeply and beautifully. Others, such as Crystal, when she was picked up from a store and taken to the Russian Emperor's villa, this clock was dragged on for at least a thousand feet, but it did not have any stiff problems. This kind of novel clock is rarely seen in American films.

As for the actors, Lilian Harvey's Crystal and Conlevert's Metternich were the best, and the others were very capable, allowing us to praise them as good.

There is also one point, at the final ending. When it was reported outside that Napoleon had landed in France, the order in the lively and joyous meeting place was disrupted, and the kings and politicians scattered, and the Russian Emperor also hastily set off, abandoning Crystal. This style was originally a characteristic of German films. I think this kind of ending is also a clever place for the director.

Tom Mix Leaves Universal

— Xue

The famous martial arts star Tom Mix has decided to completely leave the film industry. Originally, in the contract he signed with Universal Pictures, it was stated that he should act in six films for Universal, but now he has only acted in three, and he will not act in the other three. Universal Pictures is very understanding of the reasons for his departure.

Tom Mix recently announced that the environment and various circumstances forced him to retire and recuperate. He will take his wife and make up for the honeymoon trip that they have postponed to this day. After staying in Europe for a while, they also want to travel around the world.

Tom Mix has been in the film industry for twenty-four years and has acted in three hundred and seventy-four films. During the production, he has encountered twenty-five bone fractures and countless injuries. His famous horse "Tony" will also leave the screen at the same time.

How should we feel sorry and wish them good health for the retirement of this "Old Tom," the most famous and experienced person in the film industry, and his famous horse!

The Little Girl Who Was Forgotten Is Back, Jack

—

Six or seven years ago, on the stage of a Los Angeles theater, a sixteen-year-old dancer showed off her skills, attracting the attention of Chaplin. He signed a contract with this petite and unknown Irish girl and invited her to play a key role in the "Circus" comedy film. The next day, her name, Merna Kennedy, became famous in Hollywood.

Merna Kennedy had never been on camera before, and had never even been to a production studio. It was really news that she could play an important supporting role with the greatest artist on the screen.

The widely rumored Chaplin film began production, and Merna Kennedy's name spread like wildfire. Only half of the "Circus" comedy film had been made when Chaplin's wife, Lita Grey, filed for divorce. The film was temporarily put on hold, waiting for the trial of the divorce case that everyone in Hollywood was paying attention to. This divorce case had nothing to do with Merna Kennedy, but the newspapers insisted on dragging Merna into the vortex in order to get news. This sixteen-year-old girl, who was always regarded as a child by Chaplin, also became a good source of information for reporters.

The completion of the "Circus" comedy film actually became a great masterpiece for this inexperienced red-haired little dancer. Her achievements were unanimously praised by American critics. However, Hollywood was jealous of her. Her skills on the screen flashed like a meteor, and then she disappeared into obscurity.

Hollywood seemed determined to forget her, but Merna Kennedy could not be forgotten. When Lemir was making the stage play "Broadway" into a film, he abandoned a large string of established stars and chose her to play the heroine of the film. As a result, Hollywood was shocked again. At that time, she was twenty years old and secretly met enemies again. Therefore, she decided not to work unless she had the opportunity she desired. From then on, she was again unknown for two years.

Merna Kennedy deeply felt that it was not easy to rise again a second time, and it seemed that she did not have the courage to rise again a third time. But without revealing her feelings, she has now squeezed into the forefront of Hollywood stars. Her first film to rise again for the third time is Lady with a Past. She has been in Hollywood for six years and is now twenty-three years old, more beautiful than before.

Movie Emperor Charles Farrell Has Resigned

— Ren Feng

American movie emperor Charles Farrell has now officially terminated his contract with Fox Company.

He has been working at Fox Company for seven long years. His first famous masterpiece was "Seventh Heaven". Later, he and Janet Gaynor continued to produce many successful masterpieces, such as "Street Angel", "Sunrise: A Song of Two Humans", "State Fair", "The Man Who Came Back", and "The First Year", which can be said to be the crystallization of their hard work.

According to him, the director at Fox Company promoted him to play the main role in the film, so that he could develop all his talents or ambitions as much as possible. He is deeply grateful for this. However, Fox's time was used so economically that he did not have enough time to treat his "nasal disease". Although this is a minor illness, he feels that for the sake of general health, it is always appropriate to undergo surgery.

After Farrell quietly walked out of Fox Company and announced his departure, he walked into the clinic of a surgeon and asked to treat his "nasal disease". This was his first treatment.

After he left, Janet Gaynor will inevitably have to sing a solo show. Who will be the successor to Farrell in the future? This is really a big problem for Fox Company. "Tess of the Storm Country" is his and Janet's last joint masterpiece.

Marlene Dietrich's Return to Germany Scheduled

Marlene Dietrich was originally a star from the German Ufa film company. She starred in many famous films for Paramount. Her husband, Rudolf Sieber, was originally an important staff member of the German Ufa film company. He arrived in New York from Berlin on the 15th of last month and immediately transferred to Hollywood. His trip was specifically to bring a script written for Marlene by the Ufa company to his wife. At the same time, he took this opportunity to spend Christmas with his beloved wife. Ms. Dietrich is scheduled to depart for Germany around April 1st. At that time, her contract with Paramount will have expired, and Josef von Sternberg will have been working as a director at Ufa. (Note: Sternberg was previously rumored to retire, but in reality, it was a pretext to decline the employer's request. When Ufa's representative, Illek Pummer, came to the United States, he signed a contract with Ufa.)

"The Match King's" Story (16)

— Translated by Xi Meng

"Paul, I'm terribly sorry," she said softly, unwilling to hurt him, "but I must tell you... I waited for a long time, and you never came... so I..."

He looked at her face as if he was blaming her somewhat.

"What? What's wrong with you? Baby, what are you saying?"

"Paul, I'm really very sorry," she said slowly, lowering her head... She said it, looking extremely pitiful. "But I have already... already promised myself to someone else."

His face suddenly turned ashen. His age seemed to have increased by several years in an instant.

"May I... who is that person, Martha?" he asked distractedly.

"It's Chilino," she said softly.

"But I was the one who introduced you two."

"Yes. I waited for you for a long time, and he also waited for me for a long time... Later, I thought, no matter how much you love me, you will never be able to get rid of your business... And Chilino, he gave up all his career, he cancelled the contracts for concerts everywhere, he disregarded his future, regardless of everything, he came to my side... Alas, Paul, I think what you can't do, Chilino can do... but... dear... he is still waiting for me now, I will go back tonight. Next month, my film will be completed, and we will get married, and then we will return to Salzburg together."

"I hope..." Paul said, admitting defeat, "you can be very happy forever."

"Paul, you are so lovely, I understand all the suffering in your heart," she said. "How can you know!" Paul's throat was almost hoarse, and his smile was extremely unnatural. "Then you go, dear."

She took his hand. "Goodbye, Paul. Good luck to you, God be with you forever," he said softly.

"Goodbye," he said in a very low voice.

When she left, Paul collapsed into a chair. He was already a disabled man. The machine he created himself was still a slave to his own machine.

But the function of that machine has not yet been fully exerted.

Those Italian fake treasury bonds, he had already sold them on Tan Street. The big banker who accepted the treasury bonds promised him to transfer the account of forty million to a bank in Paris. So Paul took a boat east and returned to Stockholm. (To be continued)
